<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possible_stage_adaptation">Possible stage adaptation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Alice_in_Wonderland_(2010_film)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Possible stage adaptation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_Theatrical" title="Walt Disney Theatrical">Walt Disney Theatrical</a> is in early talks with Burton and screenwriter <a href="/wiki/Linda_Woolverton" title="Linda Woolverton">Linda Woolverton</a> to develop the property as a Broadway musical. Woolverton authored the screenplay for Disney's <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lion_King_(musical)" title="The Lion King (musical)">The Lion King</a></i> and is also the <a href="/wiki/Tony_Award" title="Tony Award">Tony Award</a>-nominated book writer of <i><a href="/wiki/Beauty_and_the_Beast_(musical)" title="Beauty and the Beast (musical)">Beauty and the Beast</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Aida_(musical)" title="Aida (musical)">Aida</a></i> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lestat:_The_Musical" title="Lestat: The Musical">Lestat</a></i>. Burton will also render the overall designs for the stage musical. Woolverton will adapt her screenplay for the stage production. Neither a composer nor songwriting team has been chosen yet. Direction and choreography will be done by <a href="/wiki/Rob_Ashford" title="Rob Ashford">Rob Ashford</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130"><a href="#cite_note-130"><span>[</span>130<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131"><span>[</span>131<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132"><a href="#cite_note-132"><span>[</span>132<span>]</span></a></sup> The musical is aiming to make its world-premiere in London.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133"><span>[</span>133<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sequel">Sequel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Alice_in_Wonderland_(2010_film)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Sequel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Alice_in_Wonderland:_Through_the_Looking_Glass" title="Alice in Wonderland: Through the Looking Glass">Alice in Wonderland: Through the Looking Glass</a></div>
<p>On December 7, 2012, <a href="/wiki/Variety_(magazine)" title="Variety (magazine)"><i>Variety</i></a> announced the development of a sequel to <i>Alice in Wonderland</i>, with Linda Woolverton returning to write a screenplay.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134"><span>[</span>134<span>]</span></a></sup> On May 31, 2013, <a href="/wiki/James_Bobin" title="James Bobin">James Bobin</a> began talks to direct the sequel under the working title <i>Alice in Wonderland: Into the Looking Glass.</i><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135"><span>[</span>135<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Depp" title="Johnny Depp">Johnny Depp</a> will return as <a href="/wiki/The_Hatter" title="The Hatter">the Hatter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mia_Wasikowska" title="Mia Wasikowska">Mia Wasikowska</a> will reprise the role of Alice and <a href="/wiki/Helena_Bonham_Carter" title="Helena Bonham Carter">Helena Bonham Carter</a> will return as the Red Queen.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136"><span>[</span>136<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-alice2.26Jungle_137-0"><a href="#cite_note-alice2.26Jungle-137"><span>[</span>137<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138"><span>[</span>138<span>]</span></a></sup> On November 22, 2013, it was announced that the sequel will be released on May 27, 2016 and that Bobin would direct the film. <a href="/wiki/Rhys_Ifans" title="Rhys Ifans">Rhys Ifans</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sacha_Baron_Cohen" title="Sacha Baron Cohen">Sacha Baron Cohen</a> will be featured in the film.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-alice2.26Jungle_137-1"><a href="#cite_note-alice2.26Jungle-137"><span>[</span>137<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup> On January 21, 2014, the film was retitled to <i><a href="/wiki/Alice_in_Wonderland:_Through_the_Looking_Glass" title="Alice in Wonderland: Through the Looking Glass">Alice in Wonderland: Through the Looking Glass</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141"><span>[</span>141<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<tr>
<th class="navbox-group" scope="row">Reimagining</th>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-even" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
